// from 4 AM to 5:30 AM
TIMERA = 0
while 4500 > TIMERA
    wait 30
    if
        1500 > TIMERA
    then
        set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 0@ = TIMERA
        0@ *= 20
        0@ /= 1500
        set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 12@ = 0@
    else
        if
            3000 > TIMERA
        then
            set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 1@ = TIMERA
            1@ -= 1500
            1@ *= 50
            1@ /= 1500
            add_int_lvar_to_int_lvar 1@ += 0@
            set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 12@ = 1@
        else
            set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 2@ = TIMERA
            2@ -= 3000
            2@ *= 20
            2@ /= 1500
            add_int_lvar_to_int_lvar 2@ += 1@
            set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 12@ = 2@
        end
    end
    12@ += 240 // 4 AM
    set_var_int_to_var_int 13@ = 12@
    13@ /= 60
    set_var_int_to_var_int 14@ = 13@
    14@ *= 60
    set_var_int_to_var_int 15@ = 12@
    sub_int_var_from_int_var 15@ -= 14@
    set_time_of_day 13@ 15@
end
wait 1500
fade 0 500
wait 500
fade 1 1000
set_player_control $player_char can_move 1
switch_widescreen 0
restore_camera_jumpcut
set_camera_behind_player
set_time_of_day 4@ 5@
release_weather
$allow_police_chases = 1
switch_car_generator $1860 cars_to_generate_to 101
INFOPICS_FOUND()
wait 1000

goto @INFOPICS_LOOP

:HAILACAB
script_name 'TAXIHL'
set_deatharrest_state 0
const taxi_cost = -10
const taxi_cost_minus_one = 9

:HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
wait $default_wait_time
if
    is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    $onmission == 0
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if and
    is_player_on_foot $player_char
    is_score_greater $player_char money > taxi_cost_minus_one
    not is_wanted_level_greater $player_char wanted_level > 0
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
get_player_coordinates $player_char position_to 0@ 1@ 2@
set_var_float_to_var_float 2@ = 0@
2@ += 10.0
set_var_float_to_var_float 3@ = 1@
3@ += 10.0
set_var_float_to_var_float 4@ = 2@
4@ -= 20.0
set_var_float_to_var_float 5@ = 3@
5@ -= 20.0
get_random_car_of_type_in_area_no_save $cab = get_random_car_with_actors #TAXI in_area 2@ 3@ 4@ 5@
if
    $cab == -1
then
    get_random_car_of_type_in_area_no_save $cab = get_random_car_with_actors #CABBIE in_area 2@ 3@ 4@ 5@
end
if
    $cab == -1
then
    get_random_car_of_type_in_area_no_save $cab = get_random_car_with_actors #KAUFMAN in_area 2@ 3@ 4@ 5@
end
if
    not $cab == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
get_driver_of_car 15@ = car $cab
if
    not 15@ == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
set_taxi_lights $cab 1

:HAILACAB_FOUND
wait 0
if
    is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not is_car_dead $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
get_driver_of_car 15@ = car $cab
if and
    $onmission == 0
    locate_player_on_foot_car_2d $player_char near_car $cab radius 20.0 20.0 0
    not 15@ == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_UNFOUND
if
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 4
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_FOUND

:HAILACAB_BOARD
car_set_idle $cab
set_car_cruise_speed $cab max_speed_to 0.0
set_char_wait_state $player_actor anim 16 wait_state_time 800
set_char_obj_enter_car_as_passenger $player_actor go_to_car $cab

:HAILACAB_BOARDING
wait 0
if
    is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not is_car_dead $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    $onmission == 0
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_UNBOARD
if
    not is_char_sitting_in_car $player_actor sitting_in_car $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_BOARDED
get_driver_of_car 15@ = car $cab
if and
    locate_player_on_foot_car_2d $player_char near_car $cab radius 20.0 20.0 0
    not 15@ == -1
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_UNBOARD
if
    not is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 4
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_BOARD
goto @HAILACAB_BOARDING

:HAILACAB_BOARDED
set_taxi_lights $cab 0
car_wander_randomly $cab
set_car_cruise_speed $cab max_speed_to 100.0
set_car_driving_style $cab traffic_behavior_to 3
set_fading_colour 0 0 0
fade 0 2000
wait 2000
if
    is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not is_car_dead $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    is_char_sitting_in_car $player_actor sitting_in_car $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
clear_area 0 at -258.372 -403.3983 10.1736 range 5.0
set_car_coordinates $cab at -258.372 -403.3983 10.1736
set_car_heading $cab z_angle_to 29.894
set_car_forward_speed $cab speed_instantly 20.0
car_set_idle $cab
fade 1 1000
while not is_car_stopped $cab
    if
        is_player_playing $player_char
    goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
    if
        not is_car_dead $cab
    goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
    if
        is_char_sitting_in_car $player_actor sitting_in_car $cab
    goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
    wait 0
end
set_char_obj_leave_any_car $player_actor
add_score $player_char money += taxi_cost
wait 1000
if
    is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
if
    not is_car_dead $cab
goto_if_false @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR
car_wander_randomly $cab
set_car_cruise_speed $cab max_speed_to 100.0

:HAILACAB_UNFOUND
set_taxi_lights $cab 0
goto @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR

:HAILACAB_UNBOARD
set_taxi_lights $cab 0
car_wander_randomly $cab
set_car_cruise_speed $cab max_speed_to 100.0
goto @HAILACAB_LOOKFOR

:NPCS

:NPCS_1

if and

goto_if_false @NPCS_1B

    is_player_in_zone $player_char in_zone 'STARI' // Starfish Island
goto_if_false @NPCS_1B
if
    locate_player_any_means_2d $player_char 0 -378.5385 -546.1594 radius 100.0 100.0
goto_if_false @NPCS_1B

    $npcs_diaz_state == 0

    NPCS_DIAZ_INIT()

goto_if_false @NPCS_3B
$interactions_viceport_garage_triggered = 0

then
    NPCS_VICEPORT_GARAGE_INIT()
end

:NPCS_3B

    is_player_in_area_2d $player_char 0 -873.0 -1527.0 -801.0 -1440.0

goto_if_false @NPCS_4B

goto_if_false @NPCS_5B
if
    locate_player_any_means_3d $player_char 0 257.0 27.0 12.0 radius 30.0 30.0 100.0
goto_if_false @NPCS_5B
get_time_of_day 0@ = hours, 1@ = minutes
if or
    0@ >= 23
    4 >= 0@
goto_if_false @NPCS_5B

    $music_found == 1
goto_if_false @NPCS_7B

    locate_player_in_car_3d $player_char sphere 0 near_point_in_car -221.3 -422.7 11.2 radius 2.0 2.0 2.0
then
    if

:NPCS_DIAZ_INIT
request_model #GOLFCLUB
request_model #PIZZABOX
load_special_character 1 'IGDIAZ'
while True
    if and
        has_model_loaded #GOLFCLUB
        has_model_loaded #PIZZABOX
        has_special_character_loaded 1
    then
        break
    end
    wait 0
    if or
        not is_player_playing $player_char
        not $game_saving == 0
    then
        return
    end
end
create_char $npc_diaz = create_actor_pedtype 4 model #SPECIAL01 at -378.5385 -546.1594 34.5 // -378.4412 -554.1082 39.7731
set_char_heading $npc_diaz z_angle_to 270.6989
set_char_suffers_critical_hits $npc_diaz dismemberment_possible 0
give_weapon_to_char $npc_diaz weapon 3 ammo 3000
clear_char_threat_search $npc_diaz
set_char_never_targeted $npc_diaz untargetable 1
$npc_diaz_interacted = 0
$npcs_diaz_state = 1
start_new_script @NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT
return

:NPCS_DIAZ_DESTROY
delete_char $npc_diaz
delete_object $golf_ball_1
delete_object $golf_ball_2
delete_object $golf_ball_3
delete_object $golf_ball_4
delete_object $golf_ball_5
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #GOLFCLUB
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #PIZZABOX
unload_special_character 1
clear_mission_audio 1
$npc_diaz_interacted = 0
$npcs_diaz_state = 0
return

:NPCS_DIAZ_TICK
if
    $npc_diaz_interacted == 0
then
    if
        locate_char_any_means_char_3d $player_actor near_actor $npc_diaz radius 3.0 3.0 3.0 sphere 0
    then
        clear_mission_audio 1
        load_mission_audio 'CUB4_16' as 1
        while not has_mission_audio_loaded 1
            wait 0
            if
                not is_player_playing $player_char
            then
                return
            end
        end
        set_mission_audio_position 1 location -378.5385 -546.1594 34.5
        play_mission_audio 1
        $npc_diaz_interacted = 1
    end
else
    if
        not locate_char_any_means_char_2d $player_actor near_actor $npc_diaz radius 10.0 10.0 0
    then
        $npc_diaz_interacted = 0
    end
end
return

:NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT
script_name 'NPCDIAZ'
set_deatharrest_state 0
15@ = 0
wait 1000

:NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT_LOOP
wait 100
if and
    is_player_playing $player_char
    $npcs_diaz_state == 1
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT_END
if
    not is_char_dead $npc_diaz
goto_if_false @NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT_CLEAR
if
    15@ == 0
then
    set_char_wait_state $npc_diaz anim 33 wait_state_time -1
    15@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    15@ == 1
    TIMERA >= 300
then
    mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $golf_ball_5
    set_var_int_to_var_int $golf_ball_5 = $golf_ball_4
    set_var_int_to_var_int $golf_ball_4 = $golf_ball_3
    set_var_int_to_var_int $golf_ball_3 = $golf_ball_2
    set_var_int_to_var_int $golf_ball_2 = $golf_ball_1
    get_offset_from_char_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_actor $npc_diaz offset 0.0 0.9 -0.3
    request_model #PIZZABOX
    while not has_model_loaded #PIZZABOX
        wait 0
        if and
            is_player_playing $player_char
            $npcs_diaz_state == 1
            $game_saving == 0
        goto_if_false @NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT_END
    end
    create_object_no_offset $golf_ball_1 = init_object #PIZZABOX at 0@ 1@ 2@
    set_object_collision $golf_ball_1 collision_detection 1
    set_object_dynamic $golf_ball_1 toggle_in_moving_list 1
    generate_random_float_in_range 0@ = random_float -2.0 2.0
    generate_random_float_in_range 1@ = random_float 10.0 20.0
    generate_random_float_in_range 2@ = random_float 0.0 15.0
    add_to_object_velocity $golf_ball_1 scatter 0@ 1@ 2@ // 0.0 10.0 5.0
    generate_random_int_in_range 0@ = random_int_in_ranges 750 3000
    15@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    15@ == 2
    is_int_lvar_greater_than_int_lvar TIMERA > 0@
then
    15@ = 0
end
goto @NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT_LOOP

:NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT_CLEAR

:NPC_DIAZ_SCRIPT_END
mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $npc_workers_box
terminate_this_script

:NPCS_WORKERS_INIT
request_model #BENSON
request_model #REEFER
request_model #WMYCW
request_model #BMODK
request_model #GUNBOX
request_model #WOODENBOX
request_model #BARREL2
request_model #BARREL4

:NPCS_WORKERS_INIT_LOAD
wait 0
if or
    not is_player_playing $player_char
    not $game_saving == 0
then
    return
end
if and
    has_model_loaded #BENSON
    has_model_loaded #REEFER
    has_model_loaded #WMYCW
    has_model_loaded #BMODK
goto_if_false @NPCS_WORKERS_INIT_LOAD
if and
    has_model_loaded #GUNBOX
    has_model_loaded #WOODENBOX
    has_model_loaded #BARREL2
    has_model_loaded #BARREL4
    has_model_loaded #TRAFFICCONE
goto_if_false @NPCS_WORKERS_INIT_LOAD
create_car $npc_workers_car = create_car #BENSON at -729.67 -1169.09 9.63
set_car_heading $npc_workers_car z_angle_to 111.15
pop_car_boot $npc_workers_car
create_car $npc_workers_boat = create_car #REEFER at -720.5333 -1169.814 6.0522
set_car_heading $npc_workers_boat z_angle_to 195.2337
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BENSON
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #REEFER
create_char $npc_worker_1 = create_actor_pedtype 4 model #WMYCW at -725.56 -1167.7 9.73
set_char_heading $npc_worker_1 z_angle_to 24.68
set_char_suffers_critical_hits $npc_worker_1 dismemberment_possible 0
clear_char_threat_search $npc_worker_1
set_char_never_targeted $npc_worker_1 untargetable 1
create_char $npc_worker_2 = create_actor_pedtype 4 model #BMODK at -724.73 -1167.36 9.73 // -724.18, -1167.13
set_char_heading $npc_worker_2 z_angle_to 22.48
set_char_suffers_critical_hits $npc_worker_2 dismemberment_possible 0
clear_char_threat_search $npc_worker_2
set_char_never_targeted $npc_worker_2 untargetable 1
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #WMYCW
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BMODK

:NPCS_WORKERS_DESTROY
mark_car_as_no_longer_needed $npc_workers_car

delete_char $npc_worker_1
delete_char $npc_worker_2
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BENSON
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #REEFER
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #WMYCW
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BMODK
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #GUNBOX
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #WOODENBOX
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BARREL2
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BARREL4
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #TRAFFICCONE
$npcs_workers_state = 0
return

:NPCS_WORKERS_TICK
if
    $npc_workers_interacted == 0
then
    if
        locate_char_any_means_char_3d $player_actor near_actor $npc_worker_1 radius 5.0 5.0 5.0 sphere 0
    then
        print_now 'NPCWORK' time 3000 1
        $npc_workers_interacted = 1
    end
end
return

:NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT
script_name 'NPCWORK'
set_deatharrest_state 0
const npc_worker_1_start_angle = 80.0 // 55.0
const npc_worker_1_end_angle = -22.0
const npc_worker_2_start_angle = 47.0
const npc_worker_2_end_angle = -69.0
6@ = 0
7@ = 0
15@ = 0
wait 1000
TIMERA = 0

:NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_LOOP
wait 0
if and
    is_player_playing $player_char
    $npcs_workers_state == 1
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_END
if and
    not is_car_dead $npc_workers_car
    not is_car_dead $npc_workers_boat
    not is_char_dead $npc_worker_1
    not is_char_dead $npc_worker_2
goto_if_false @NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_CLEAR
if
    10 >= 6@
goto_if_false @NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_LEAVE
if and
    locate_car_2d $npc_workers_car sphere 0 near_point -729.67 -1169.09 radius 3.0 3.0
    locate_car_2d $npc_workers_boat sphere 0 near_point -720.5333 -1169.814 radius 3.0 3.0
goto_if_false @NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_CLEAR
if
    15@ == 0
then
    set_char_heading $npc_worker_1 z_angle_to npc_worker_1_start_angle
    set_char_wait_state $npc_worker_1 anim 25 wait_state_time 3000
    15@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    15@ == 1
    TIMERA >= 500
then
    get_offset_from_char_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_actor $npc_worker_1 offset 0.0 0.9 0.0
    14@ = #GUNBOX
    generate_random_float_in_range 13@ = random_float 0.0 1.0
    if
        13@ > 0.2
    then
        14@ = #WOODENBOX
    end
    if
        13@ > 0.4
    then
        14@ = #BARREL2
    end
    if
        13@ > 0.6
    then
        14@ = #BARREL4
    end
    if
        13@ > 0.8
    then
        14@ = #TRAFFICCONE
    end
    request_model 14@
    while not has_model_loaded 14@
        wait 0
        if and
            is_player_playing $player_char
            $npcs_workers_state == 1
            $game_saving == 0
        goto_if_false @NPC_WORKERS_SCRIPT_END
    end
    create_object_no_offset $npc_workers_box = init_object 14@ at 0@ 1@ 2@
    dont_remove_object $npc_workers_box
    15@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    15@ == 2
    TIMERA >= 500
then
    set_char_wait_state $npc_worker_2 anim 25 wait_state_time 3000
    15@++
    TIMERA = -200
end
if and
    15@ == 3
    TIMERA >= 0
then
    set_char_heading $npc_worker_2 z_angle_to npc_worker_2_start_angle
    cset_lvar_float_to_lvar_int 4@ = integer_to_float TIMERA
    4@ /= 1100.0
    4@ *= 180.0
    cos 4@ = cosine 4@
    4@ += 1.0
    4@ /= 2.0
    5@ = 1.0
    sub_float_var_from_float_var 5@ -= 4@
    3@ = npc_worker_1_end_angle
    3@ -= npc_worker_1_start_angle
    mult_float_lvar_by_float_lvar 3@ *= 5@
    3@ += npc_worker_1_start_angle
    set_char_heading $npc_worker_1 z_angle_to 3@
    get_offset_from_char_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_actor $npc_worker_1 offset 0.0 0.9 0.0
    set_object_coordinates $npc_workers_box at 0@ 1@ 2@
    if
        TIMERA >= 1100
    then
        15@++
        TIMERA = 0
    end
end
if
    15@ == 4
then
    clear_all_char_anims $npc_worker_1
    15@++
end
if
    15@ == 5
then
    cset_lvar_float_to_lvar_int 4@ = integer_to_float TIMERA
    4@ /= 500.0
    3@ = npc_worker_2_end_angle
    3@ -= npc_worker_2_start_angle
    mult_float_lvar_by_float_lvar 3@ *= 4@
    3@ += npc_worker_2_start_angle

    set_object_coordinates $npc_workers_box at 0@ 1@ 2@
    if
        TIMERA >= 500
    then
        set_object_dynamic $npc_workers_box toggle_in_moving_list 1

        0@ += 0.0

        mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $npc_workers_box
        15@++
        TIMERA = 0
    end
end

    15@ == 6
    TIMERA >= 600
then
    clear_all_char_anims $npc_worker_2
    generate_random_int_in_range 0@ = random_int_in_ranges 0 200
    15@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    15@ == 7
    is_int_lvar_greater_than_int_lvar TIMERA > 0@
then
    15@ = 0
    6@++
end

    7@ == 0

    then
        if
            locate_player_any_means_car_3d $player_char near_car $npc_lovefist_car radius 10.0 10.0 10.0 unknown 0
        then
            clear_mission_audio 1
            load_mission_audio 'PSYCH_2' as 1
            while not has_mission_audio_loaded 1
                wait 0
                if
                    not is_player_playing $player_char
                then
                    return
                end
            end
            get_char_coordinates $npc_lovefist_7 position_to 0@ 1@ 2@
            set_mission_audio_position 1 location 0@ 1@ 2@
            play_mission_audio 1
            $npc_lovefist_interacted = 1
        end
    end
    if
        not is_car_health_greater $npc_lovefist_car health > 249
    then
        set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe $npc_lovefist_1
        set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe $npc_lovefist_2
        set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe $npc_lovefist_3
        set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe $npc_lovefist_4
        set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe $npc_lovefist_5
        set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe $npc_lovefist_6
        set_char_obj_flee_on_foot_till_safe $npc_lovefist_7
    end
end
return

    set_char_personality $npc_biker_2 ped_stats_to 11
    set_char_personality $npc_biker_3 ped_stats_to 11
    set_char_suffers_critical_hits $npc_biker_2 dismemberment_possible 0
    set_char_suffers_critical_hits $npc_biker_3 dismemberment_possible 0
    set_char_never_targeted $npc_biker_2 untargetable 1
    set_char_never_targeted $npc_biker_3 untargetable 1
    turn_char_to_face_char $npc_biker_2 $npc_biker_3
    turn_char_to_face_char $npc_biker_3 $npc_biker_2
    set_char_wait_state $npc_biker_2 anim 19 wait_state_time 9999999
    set_char_wait_state $npc_biker_3 anim 19 wait_state_time 9999999
end
$npcs_bikers_state = 1
return

:NPCS_BIKERS_CREATE_GUARD
create_char $npc_biker_1 = create_actor_pedtype 4 model #BKB at -600.1636 652.1155 10.1262
set_char_heading $npc_biker_1 z_angle_to 0.0
set_char_health $npc_biker_1 health_to 150
clear_char_threat_search $npc_biker_1
set_char_heed_threats $npc_biker_1 heed_threats 1
set_char_personality $npc_biker_1 ped_stats_to 11
set_char_suffers_critical_hits $npc_biker_1 dismemberment_possible 0
set_char_never_targeted $npc_biker_1 untargetable 1
return

:NPCS_BIKERS_DESTROY
remove_char_elegantly $npc_biker_1
remove_char_elegantly $npc_biker_2
remove_char_elegantly $npc_biker_3
$npcs_bikers_state = 0
return

//-------------Random interactions---------------
//

:INTERACTIONS
script_name 'INTERAC'
set_deatharrest_state 0
$interactions_golf_barrels_state = 0
$interactions_viceport_garage_triggered = 0

:INTERACTIONS_UNDEF
if or
    not is_player_playing $player_char
    not $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_1
wait 0
goto @INTERACTIONS_UNDEF

:INTERACTIONS_1
wait 0
if and
    is_player_playing $player_char
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_1B
if or
    is_player_in_zone $player_char in_zone 'GOLFC' // Leaf Links
    is_player_in_zone $player_char in_zone 'BEACH3' // Vice Point
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_1B
if or
    locate_player_any_means_2d $player_char 0 164.7667 252.5675 radius 100.0 100.0
    locate_player_any_means_2d $player_char 0 52.3614 200.3506 radius 100.0 100.0
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_1B
if
    $interactions_golf_barrels_state == 0
then
    INTERACTIONS_GOLF_BARRELS_INIT()
    goto @INTERACTIONS_1
end
if
    $interactions_golf_barrels_state == 1
then
    INTERACTIONS_GOLF_BARRELS_TICK()
end
goto @INTERACTIONS_2

:INTERACTIONS_1B
if
    $interactions_golf_barrels_state > 0
then
    INTERACTIONS_GOLF_BARRELS_DESTROY()
end

:INTERACTIONS_2
if and
    is_player_playing $player_char
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_2C
if
    is_player_in_zone $player_char in_zone 'DOCKS' // Viceport
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_2C
if
    is_player_in_area_2d $player_char 0 -841.0 -1488.0 -820.0 -1475.0
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_2C
if
    $interactions_viceport_garage_triggered == 0
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_2B
if
    is_player_pressing_horn $player_char
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_3
$interactions_viceport_garage_triggered = 10
goto @INTERACTIONS_3

:INTERACTIONS_2B
if
    $interactions_viceport_garage_triggered == 10
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_3
if
    not is_player_pressing_horn $player_char
goto_if_false @INTERACTIONS_3
$interactions_viceport_garage_triggered = 1
goto @INTERACTIONS_3

:INTERACTIONS_2C
$interactions_viceport_garage_triggered = 0

:INTERACTIONS_3
goto @INTERACTIONS_1

:INTERACTIONS_GOLF_BARRELS_INIT
request_model #BARREL4
while not has_model_loaded #BARREL4
    wait 0
    if or
        not is_player_playing $player_char
        not $game_saving == 0
    then
        return
    end
end
create_object $golf_barrel_1 = create_object #BARREL4 at 164.77 252.57 18.33
create_object $golf_barrel_2 = create_object #BARREL4 at 163.77 251.2 18.29
create_object $golf_barrel_3 = create_object #BARREL4 at 165.84 251.49 18.28
create_object $golf_barrel_4 = create_object #BARREL4 at 52.36 200.35 18.23
create_object $golf_barrel_5 = create_object #BARREL4 at 54.71 200.99 18.17
create_object $golf_barrel_6 = create_object #BARREL4 at 54.61 200.94 19.27
make_object_targetable $golf_barrel_1
make_object_targetable $golf_barrel_2
make_object_targetable $golf_barrel_3
make_object_targetable $golf_barrel_4
make_object_targetable $golf_barrel_5
make_object_targetable $golf_barrel_6
dont_remove_object $golf_barrel_1
dont_remove_object $golf_barrel_2
dont_remove_object $golf_barrel_3
dont_remove_object $golf_barrel_4
dont_remove_object $golf_barrel_5
dont_remove_object $golf_barrel_6
$interactions_golf_barrels_state = 1
return

:INTERACTIONS_GOLF_BARRELS_DESTROY
delete_object $golf_barrel_1
delete_object $golf_barrel_2
delete_object $golf_barrel_3
delete_object $golf_barrel_4
delete_object $golf_barrel_5
delete_object $golf_barrel_6
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BARREL4
if
    $interactions_golf_barrels_state > 1
then
    delete_object $1821
    create_object_no_offset $1821 = init_object #GOLF_GATESCLOSED at 107.671 227.729 20.634
    dont_remove_object $1821
end
$interactions_golf_barrels_state = 0
return

:INTERACTIONS_GOLF_BARRELS_TICK
if or
    has_object_been_damaged $golf_barrel_1
    has_object_been_damaged $golf_barrel_2
    has_object_been_damaged $golf_barrel_3
    has_object_been_damaged $golf_barrel_4
    has_object_been_damaged $golf_barrel_5
    has_object_been_damaged $golf_barrel_6
    locate_player_any_means_3d $player_char 0 95.8965 264.4538 21.7719 radius 5.0 5.0 5.0
    locate_player_any_means_3d $player_char 0 81.1972 241.7551 23.5315 radius 3.0 3.0 3.0
then
    mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $golf_barrel_1
    mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $golf_barrel_2
    mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $golf_barrel_3
    mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $golf_barrel_4
    mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $golf_barrel_5
    mark_object_as_no_longer_needed $golf_barrel_6
    delete_object $1821
    create_object_no_offset $1821 = init_object #GOLF_GATESOPEN at 107.81 228.072 20.989
    dont_remove_object $1821
    $interactions_golf_barrels_state = 2
end
return

//-------------Player drops money when wasted---------------
//

:DROPMONEY
script_name 'DROPMON'
set_deatharrest_state 0
$dropped_money_pickups_exist = 1

:DROPMONEY_LOOP
wait $default_wait_time
if
    not is_player_playing $player_char
then
    if
        $dropped_money_pickups_exist == 1
    then
        DROPMONEY_DESTROYPICKUPS()
    end
    goto @DROPMONEY_LOOP
end
if
    not is_player_health_greater $player_char health > 0
goto_if_false @DROPMONEY_LOOP
if
    $dropped_money_pickups_exist == 1
then
    DROPMONEY_DESTROYPICKUPS()
end
get_dead_char_pickup_coords $player_actor store_to 0@ 1@ 2@
get_dead_char_pickup_coords $player_actor store_to 3@ 4@ 5@
get_dead_char_pickup_coords $player_actor store_to 6@ 7@ 8@
get_dead_char_pickup_coords $player_actor store_to 9@ 10@ 11@
get_dead_char_pickup_coords $player_actor store_to 12@ 13@ 14@
create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_1 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 0@ 1@ 2@
create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_2 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 3@ 4@ 5@
create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_3 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 6@ 7@ 8@
create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_4 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 9@ 10@ 11@
create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_5 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 12@ 13@ 14@

:DROPMONEY_WAIT
wait 0
if
    not is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @DROPMONEY_WAIT

:DROPMONEY_WAIT_2
wait 0
if
    is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @DROPMONEY_WAIT_2
if
    has_pickup_been_collected $player_dropped_cash_1
then
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_1
else
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_1
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_1 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 0@ 1@ 2@
end
if
    has_pickup_been_collected $player_dropped_cash_2
then
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_2
else
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_2
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_2 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 3@ 4@ 5@
end
if
    has_pickup_been_collected $player_dropped_cash_3
then
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_3
else
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_3
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_3 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 6@ 7@ 8@
end
if
    has_pickup_been_collected $player_dropped_cash_4
then
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_4
else
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_4
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_4 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 9@ 10@ 11@
end
if
    has_pickup_been_collected $player_dropped_cash_5
then
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_5
else
    remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_5
    create_money_pickup $player_dropped_cash_5 = create_cash_pickup 20 at 12@ 13@ 14@
end
goto @DROPMONEY_LOOP

:DROPMONEY_DESTROYPICKUPS
remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_1
remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_2
remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_3
remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_4
remove_pickup $player_dropped_cash_5
$dropped_money_pickups_exist = 0
return

//-------------Police chases on streets---------------
//

:POLICE_CHASES
script_name 'PCHASES'
set_deatharrest_state 0
start_new_script @POLICE_CHASES_A
start_new_script @POLICE_CHASES_B
start_new_script @POLICE_CHASES_C
start_new_script @POLICE_CHASES_D
start_new_script @POLICE_CHASES_E
terminate_this_script
const pc_gang_1_model = 4@ // transient
const pc_gang_2_model = 5@ // transient
// pc_cop_1..pc_gang_2 may get rewritten before the actors are created
const pc_cop_1 = 6@
const pc_cop_2 = 7@
const pc_cop_3 = 8@
const pc_gang_1 = 9@
const pc_gang_2 = 10@
const pc_police_car_1 = 11@
const pc_police_car_2 = 12@
const pc_gang_car = 13@
const pc_gang_car_model = 14@
const pc_step = 15@
const police_chase_spawn_distance = 150.0
const police_chase_min_spawn_distance = 100.0
const police_chase_despawn_distance = 200.0
const police_chases_police_car_start_health = 1500
const police_chases_gang_car_start_health = 1500
const police_chases_police_car_max_speed = 30.0
const police_chases_gang_car_max_speed = 25.0
const police_chases_two_police_cars_chance = 0.5
const police_chases_on_foot_fight_chance = 0.5
const police_chases_weapon_accuracy_in_car = 50
const police_chases_weapon_accuracy_on_foot = 50

:POLICE_CHASES_A
script_name 'PCHASEA'
set_deatharrest_state 0
pc_gang_car_model = #ADMIRAL
pc_step = 0
goto @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT

:POLICE_CHASES_B
script_name 'PCHASEB'
set_deatharrest_state 0
pc_gang_car_model = #GANGBUR
pc_step = 0
goto @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT

:POLICE_CHASES_C
script_name 'PCHASEC'
set_deatharrest_state 0
pc_gang_car_model = #CUBAN
pc_step = 0
goto @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT

:POLICE_CHASES_D
script_name 'PCHASED'
set_deatharrest_state 0
pc_gang_car_model = #CUBAN
pc_step = 0
goto @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT

:POLICE_CHASES_E
script_name 'PCHASEE'
set_deatharrest_state 0
pc_gang_car_model = #ADMIRAL
pc_step = 1000 // only spawn in the night hours
goto @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT

:POLICE_CHASES_SET_GANG_MODELS
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #ADMIRAL
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #CLA
    pc_gang_2_model = #CLB
end
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #GANGBUR
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #CLA
    pc_gang_2_model = #CLB
end
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #CUBAN
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #CBA
    pc_gang_2_model = #CBB
end
if
    pc_gang_car_model == #VOODOO
then
    pc_gang_1_model = #HNA
    pc_gang_2_model = #HNB
end
return

:POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
wait $default_wait_time
if and
    is_player_playing $player_char
    $allow_police_chases == 1
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
get_time_of_day 0@ = hours, 1@ = minutes
if
    pc_step == 1000
then
    if
        2 >= 0@
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
else
    if or
        0@ >= 21
        4 >= 0@
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

generate_random_int_in_range 0@ = random_int_in_ranges 1000 60000
TIMERA = 0
while is_int_lvar_greater_than_int_lvar 0@ > TIMERA
    wait $default_wait_time
    if and
        is_player_playing $player_char
        $allow_police_chases == 1
        $game_saving == 0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

TIMERA = 0
while 10000 > TIMERA
    get_player_coordinates $player_char position_to 4@ 5@ 6@
    generate_random_float_in_range 3@ = random_float 0.0 360.0
    sin 0@ = sine 3@
    0@ *= police_chase_spawn_distance
    add_float_var_to_float_var 0@ += 4@
    cos 1@ = cosine 3@
    1@ *= police_chase_spawn_distance
    add_float_var_to_float_var 1@ += 5@
    get_closest_car_node_with_heading 0@ 1@ 2@ store_nearby_vector_to 0@ 1@ 2@ 3@
    get_distance_between_coords_2d 6@ = distance_between_point 4@ 5@ and_point 0@ 1@
    if
        6@ > police_chase_min_spawn_distance
    then
        if or // outside of Leaf Links
            -300.0 > 0@
            0@ > 300.0
            -250.0 > 1@
            1@ > 650.0
        then
            break
        end
    end
    wait $default_wait_time
    if and
        is_player_playing $player_char
        $allow_police_chases == 1
        $game_saving == 0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

// there's no opcode to check if a point is in an info zone
4@ = 0 // 1 = Little Havana; 2 = Little Haiti
if and
    -1208.21 < 0@
    0@ < -748.206
    -898.738 < 1@
    1@ < -241.467
then
    4@ = 1
end
if and
    -1208.21 < 0@
    0@ < -578.289
    -241.467 < 1@
    1@ < 412.66
then
    4@ = 2
end
if
    4@ > 0
then
    if or
        pc_gang_car_model == #CUBAN
        pc_gang_car_model == #VOODOO
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
    if
        4@ == 2
    then
        pc_gang_car_model = #VOODOO
    else
        pc_gang_car_model = #CUBAN
    end
else
    if and
        not pc_gang_car_model == #CUBAN
        not pc_gang_car_model == #VOODOO
    goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
end

POLICE_CHASES_SET_GANG_MODELS()
request_model #POLICE
request_model #COP
request_model #UZI
request_model #MP5LNG
request_model pc_gang_car_model
request_model pc_gang_1_model
request_model pc_gang_2_model

:POLICE_CHASES_LOAD
if or
    not has_model_loaded #POLICE
    not has_model_loaded #COP
    not has_model_loaded #UZI
    not has_model_loaded #MP5LNG
    not has_model_loaded pc_gang_car_model
    not has_model_loaded pc_gang_1_model
    not has_model_loaded pc_gang_2_model
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_LOADED
wait 0
if and
    is_player_playing $player_char
    $allow_police_chases == 1
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_WAIT
goto @POLICE_CHASES_LOAD

:POLICE_CHASES_LOADED
create_car pc_police_car_1 = create_car #POLICE at 0@ 1@ 2@
set_car_heading pc_police_car_1 z_angle_to 3@
get_offset_from_car_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_car pc_police_car_1 offset 0.0 7.0 0.0
create_car pc_gang_car = create_car pc_gang_car_model at 0@ 1@ 2@
set_car_heading pc_gang_car z_angle_to 3@
pc_police_car_2 = 0
pc_cop_3 = 0
generate_random_float_in_range 0@ = random_float 0.0 1.0
if
    police_chases_two_police_cars_chance > 0@
then
    get_offset_from_car_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_car pc_police_car_1 offset 0.0 -7.0 0.0
    create_car pc_police_car_2 = create_car #POLICE at 0@ 1@ 2@
    set_car_heading pc_police_car_2 z_angle_to 3@
end

set_car_health pc_police_car_1 health_to police_chases_police_car_start_health
set_car_health pc_gang_car health_to police_chases_gang_car_start_health
//set_can_burst_car_tyres pc_police_car_1 tires_vulnerable 0
//set_can_burst_car_tyres pc_gang_car tires_vulnerable 0
add_upsidedown_car_check pc_police_car_1
add_upsidedown_car_check pc_gang_car
add_stuck_car_check pc_police_car_1 distance 0.5 time 3000
add_stuck_car_check pc_gang_car distance 0.5 time 3000
create_char_inside_car pc_cop_1 = create_actor 4 #COP in_car pc_police_car_1
create_char_inside_car pc_gang_1 = create_actor 4 pc_gang_1_model in_car pc_gang_car
clear_char_threat_search pc_cop_1
clear_char_threat_search pc_gang_1
set_char_personality pc_cop_1 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_personality pc_gang_1 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_cop_1 dismemberment_possible 0
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_gang_1 dismemberment_possible 0
set_char_running pc_cop_1 running 1
set_char_running pc_gang_1 running 1
set_char_health pc_cop_1 health_to 200
set_char_health pc_gang_1 health_to 200
set_car_cruise_speed pc_police_car_1 max_speed_to police_chases_police_car_max_speed
set_car_cruise_speed pc_gang_car max_speed_to police_chases_gang_car_max_speed
set_car_driving_style pc_police_car_1 traffic_behavior_to 2
set_car_driving_style pc_gang_car traffic_behavior_to 2
switch_car_siren pc_police_car_1 siren = 1
set_car_ram_car pc_police_car_1 ram pc_gang_car
car_wander_randomly pc_gang_car
if
    not is_car_dead pc_police_car_2
then
    set_car_health pc_police_car_2 health_to police_chases_police_car_start_health
    //set_can_burst_car_tyres pc_police_car_2 tires_vulnerable 0
    add_upsidedown_car_check pc_police_car_2
    add_stuck_car_check pc_police_car_2 distance 0.5 time 3000
    create_char_inside_car pc_cop_3 = create_actor 4 #COP in_car pc_police_car_2
    clear_char_threat_search pc_cop_3
    set_char_personality pc_cop_3 ped_stats_to 16
    set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_cop_3 dismemberment_possible 0
    set_char_running pc_cop_3 running 1
    set_char_health pc_cop_3 health_to 200
    set_car_cruise_speed pc_police_car_2 max_speed_to police_chases_police_car_max_speed
    set_car_driving_style pc_police_car_2 traffic_behavior_to 2
    switch_car_siren pc_police_car_2 siren = 1
    set_car_ram_car pc_police_car_2 ram pc_gang_car
end

create_char pc_cop_2 = create_actor_pedtype 4 model #COP at 0.0 0.0 0.0
create_char pc_gang_2 = create_actor_pedtype 4 model pc_gang_2_model at 0.0 0.0 0.0
clear_char_threat_search pc_cop_2
clear_char_threat_search pc_gang_2
set_char_personality pc_cop_2 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_personality pc_gang_2 ped_stats_to 16
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_cop_2 dismemberment_possible 0
set_char_suffers_critical_hits pc_gang_2 dismemberment_possible 0
attach_char_to_car pc_cop_2 into_turret_on_car pc_police_car_1 at_car_offset 0.5 0.0 0.8 position 0 angle 180.0 with_weapon 25
attach_char_to_car pc_gang_2 into_turret_on_car pc_gang_car at_car_offset 0.5 0.0 0.8 position 2 angle 180.0 with_weapon 23
set_char_accuracy pc_cop_2 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_in_car
set_char_accuracy pc_gang_2 weapon_accuracy_to police_chases_weapon_accuracy_in_car
set_char_health pc_cop_2 health_to 200
set_char_health pc_gang_2 health_to 200
set_char_obj_destroy_car pc_cop_2 destroy_car pc_gang_car
set_char_obj_destroy_car pc_gang_2 destroy_car pc_police_car_1

mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #POLICE
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #COP
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed pc_gang_car_model
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed pc_gang_1_model
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed pc_gang_2_model
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #UZI
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #MP5LNG

1@ = 0 // on foot fight enabled
generate_random_float_in_range 0@ = random_float 0.0 1.0
if
    police_chases_on_foot_fight_chance > 0@
then
    1@ = 1 // will get overwritten for pc_step > 0
end

:POLICE_CHASES_LOOP
wait $default_wait_time
if and
    is_player_playing $player_char
    $allow_police_chases == 1
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_DESTROY
if
    $game_saving == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_CHASES_ABANDON

        not is_car_health_greater pc_gang_car health > 400

:REPAINT
script_name 'REPAINT'
set_deatharrest_state 0
$repaint_garage_open = 0
const repaint_cost = -200
const repaint_cost_minus_one = 199

:REPAINT_WAIT
wait $default_wait_time
if
    is_player_playing $player_char
goto_if_false @REPAINT_WAIT
if and
    is_player_in_zone $player_char in_zone 'HAVANA' // Little Havana
    $onmission == 0
goto_if_false @REPAINT_WAIT
if
    $repaint_garage_open == 0
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_2d $player_char 0 -1009.0 -837.0 radius 15.0 15.0
    then
        open_garage $682
        $repaint_garage_open = 1
    end
else
    if
        not locate_player_any_means_2d $player_char 0 -1009.0 -837.0 radius 15.0 15.0
    then
        close_garage $682
        $repaint_garage_open = 0
    end
end
if and
    is_player_stopped_in_area_in_car_3d $player_char 0 -1014.341 -857.732 6.325 -1001.315 -841.532 10.885
    can_player_start_mission $player_char
goto_if_false @REPAINT_WAIT
if
    not is_score_greater $player_char money > repaint_cost_minus_one
then
    0@ = 0
    0@ -= repaint_cost
    print_with_number 'PAINTNO' 0@ time 250 1
    jump @REPAINT_WAIT
end
set_player_control $player_char can_move 0
print_help_forever 'PAINT'
store_car_player_is_in_no_save 11@ = player $player_char
get_car_colours 11@ color 12@ 13@
set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 14@ = 12@
set_lvar_int_to_lvar_int 15@ = 13@
set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 1500
set_fixed_camera_position -1002.842 -842.3333 10.365 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
point_camera_at_car 11@ mode 15 switchstyle 1
0@ = 0

:REPAINT_KEYUP
if or
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 14
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 16
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 10
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 11
goto_if_false @REPAINT_PROCESS
wait 0
jump @REPAINT_KEYUP

:REPAINT_PROCESS
wait 0
print_with_2_numbers_now 'PAINT2' 14@ 15@ time 50 1
if
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 14
then
    0@ = 1
    goto @REPAINT_CHANGE
end
if

    while 15@ > 59
        15@ -= 60
        14@++
    end

POLICE_1_CLEANUP()
terminate_this_script

:POLICE_1_START
$onmission = 1
$allow_police_chases = 0
set_fading_colour 0 0 0
register_mission_given
load_mission_text 'POLICE1'
set_player_control $player_char can_move 0
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 1
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 1
request_model #BOBCAT
request_model #POLICE
request_model #VICE3
fade 0 500
wait 500

:POLICE_1_LOAD
wait 0
if and
    has_model_loaded #BOBCAT
    has_model_loaded #POLICE
    has_model_loaded #VICE3
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_LOAD
clear_area 0 at 333.704 -501.9003 9.7059 range 50.0
set_car_density_multiplier 0.0
set_ped_density_multiplier 0.0
create_car $objective_car = create_car #BOBCAT at 332.4361 -512.1122 8.9081
set_car_heading $objective_car z_angle_to 96.6302
change_car_colour $objective_car color_to 67 8
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BOBCAT
set_can_burst_car_tyres $objective_car tires_vulnerable 0
create_car 0@ = create_car #POLICE at 359.5053 -514.6687 11.961
set_car_heading 0@ z_angle_to 322.4988
create_char_inside_car 1@ = create_actor 4 #VICE3 in_car 0@
car_set_idle 0@
set_car_only_damaged_by_player 0@ immune_to_nonplayer 1
set_car_temp_action 0@ action 2 time 1700
switch_widescreen 1
set_fixed_camera_position 364.6485 -526.3016 13.954 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
point_camera_at_point 354.3607 -523.9194 10.0632 switchstyle 2
set_player_coordinates $player_char at 348.0225 -524.783 8.9363
set_player_heading $player_char z_angle_to 237.081
fade 1 500
if
    $mission_debug == 0
then
    wait 1700
end
set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 1500
set_fixed_camera_position 345.452 -527.0284 9.0841 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
point_camera_at_point 350.2682 -525.0466 9.9611 switchstyle 1
set_char_obj_leave_car 1@ leave_car 0@
TIMERB = 0
while is_char_in_any_car 1@
    if
        TIMERB > 5000
    then
        get_car_coordinates 0@ position_to 13@ 14@ 15@
        15@ += 1.0
        warp_char_from_car_to_coord 1@ at 13@ 14@ 15@
        break
    end
    wait 0
end
turn_char_to_face_char $player_actor look_at_actor 1@
turn_char_to_face_char 1@ look_at_actor $player_actor
set_char_wait_state 1@ anim 19 wait_state_time 20000
print_now 'INTRO1' time 5000 2
TIMERA = 0
$scene_step = 0
if
    $mission_debug == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_INTRO_END

:POLICE_1_INTRO_LOOP
wait 0
if or
    {$I incl.anykey.txt}
then
    goto @POLICE_1_INTRO_END
end

if and
    $scene_step == 0
    TIMERA >= 5000
then
    $scene_step++
    TIMERA = 0
    print_now 'INTRO2' time 4000 2
end

if and
    $scene_step == 1
    TIMERA >= 4000
then
    $scene_step++
    TIMERA = 0
    print_now 'INTRO3' time 6000 2
    set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 4000
    set_fixed_camera_position 328.5136 -520.5809 10.055 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
    point_camera_at_car $objective_car mode 15 switchstyle 1
end

if and
    $scene_step == 2
    TIMERA >= 6000
then
    goto @POLICE_1_INTRO_END
end
goto @POLICE_1_INTRO_LOOP

:POLICE_1_INTRO_END
fade 0 1000
wait 1000
clear_prints
delete_car 0@
delete_char 1@
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #POLICE
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #VICE3
request_model #WALTON
while not has_model_loaded #WALTON
    wait 0
end
create_car $mission_car = create_car #WALTON at -842.0252 -623.7845 10.0005
set_car_heading $mission_car z_angle_to 184.3139
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #WALTON
freeze_car_position $mission_car in_current_position 1
1@ = 0
set_player_coordinates $player_char 343.2275 -527.6896 9.0558
set_player_heading $player_char 30.5183
set_player_control $player_char can_move 1
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 0
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 0
set_car_density_multiplier 1.0
set_ped_density_multiplier 1.0
switch_widescreen 0
restore_camera_jumpcut
set_camera_behind_player
add_blip_for_car $objective_car_marker = create_marker_above_car $objective_car
fade 1 1000
wait 1000
print_now 'GETIN' time 5000 2
if
    $mission_debug == 1
then
    warp_char_into_car $player_actor in_car $objective_car
    set_car_coordinates $objective_car at -841.9927 -632.9435 10.8985
    wait 2000
end
0@ = 0

:POLICE_1_TRAVEL
wait 0
if
    not is_car_dead $objective_car
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_WRECKED
if
    not is_car_dead $mission_car
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_WHY
if
    1@ == 0
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car $mission_car radius 50.0 50.0 0
    then
        freeze_car_position $mission_car in_current_position 0
        1@ = 1
    end
end
if
    0@ == 0
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car $objective_car radius 35.0 35.0 0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_1_ABANDONED
    if
        is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $objective_car
    then
        remove_blip $objective_car_marker
        add_blip_for_coord $objective_point_marker = create_checkpoint_at -842.6732 -632.8707 10.9397
        print_now 'TRAVEL' time 5000 2
        0@ = 1
    end
else
    if
        not is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $objective_car
    then
        print_now 'GETBACK' time 5000 2
        remove_blip $objective_point_marker
        add_blip_for_car $objective_car_marker = create_marker_above_car $objective_car
        0@ = 0
    else
        if
            not locate_stopped_player_in_car_3d $player_char stopped 1 -842.6732 -632.8707 10.9397 radius 4.0 4.0 3.0
        goto_if_false @POLICE_1_TRAVEL_END
    end
end
goto @POLICE_1_TRAVEL

:POLICE_1_TRAVEL_END
set_player_control $player_char can_move 0
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 1
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 1
clear_prints
remove_blip $objective_point_marker
request_model #POLICE
request_model #WMYPI
request_model #COP
request_model #GUNBOX
request_model #CARDBOARDBOX2
load_special_character 2 'S_KEEP'
fade 0 500
wait 500
while true
    wait 0
    if and
        has_model_loaded #POLICE
        has_model_loaded #WMYPI
        has_model_loaded #COP
        has_model_loaded #GUNBOX
        has_model_loaded #CARDBOARDBOX2
        has_special_character_loaded 2
    then
        break
    end
end
switch_widescreen 1
set_fixed_camera_position -857.2355 -645.65 10.7089 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
point_camera_at_point -848.9108 -643.3928 11.6605 switchstyle 2
clear_area 0 at -843.4048 -634.9933 9.9503 range 50.0
set_car_density_multiplier 0.0
set_ped_density_multiplier 0.0
warp_player_from_car_to_coord $player_char at -842.8207 -628.7374 11.1047
turn_char_to_face_coord $player_actor to_look_at_spot -843.4048 -634.9933 9.9503
set_car_coordinates $objective_car at -843.4048 -634.9933 9.9503
set_car_heading $objective_car z_angle_to 188.753
boat_stop $objective_car
set_car_coordinates $mission_car at -842.0252 -623.7845 10.1005
set_car_heading $mission_car z_angle_to 184.3139
create_object $mission_obj_1 = create_object #GUNBOX at 0.0 0.0 0.0
create_object $mission_obj_2 = create_object #CARDBOARDBOX2 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
create_object $mission_obj_3 = create_object #CARDBOARDBOX2 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
create_object $mission_obj_4 = create_object #GUNBOX at 0.0 0.0 0.0
create_object $mission_obj_5 = create_object #CARDBOARDBOX2 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
set_object_collision $mission_obj_1 collision_detection 0
set_object_collision $mission_obj_2 collision_detection 0
set_object_collision $mission_obj_3 collision_detection 0
set_object_collision $mission_obj_4 collision_detection 0
set_object_collision $mission_obj_5 collision_detection 0
set_object_dynamic $mission_obj_1 toggle_in_moving_list 0
set_object_dynamic $mission_obj_2 toggle_in_moving_list 0
set_object_dynamic $mission_obj_3 toggle_in_moving_list 0
set_object_dynamic $mission_obj_4 toggle_in_moving_list 0
set_object_dynamic $mission_obj_5 toggle_in_moving_list 0
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_1 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.45 -0.85 0.25
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_2 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.4 -0.95 0.2
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_3 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.35 -1.65 0.15
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_4 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.45 -1.85 0.3
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_5 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.0 -1.1 0.9
create_char $mission_actor_1 = create_actor_pedtype 4 model #SPECIAL02 at -844.87 -629.8369 10.1341
set_char_heading $mission_actor_1 z_angle_to 208.6404
clear_char_threat_search $mission_actor_1
unload_special_character 2
create_char $mission_actor_2 = create_actor_pedtype 4 model #WMYPI at -846.0 -635.0 16.0
set_char_heading $mission_actor_2 z_angle_to 270.0
clear_char_threat_search $mission_actor_2
set_char_proofs $mission_actor_2 immunities BP 1 FP 1 EP 1 CP 1 MP 1
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #WMYPI
create_car $mission_car_2 = create_car #POLICE at -781.5236 -920.9225 9.0674
set_car_heading $mission_car_2 z_angle_to 70.2566
switch_car_siren $mission_car_2 siren = 1
create_char_inside_car $mission_actor_3 = create_actor 4 #COP in_car $mission_car_2
freeze_car_position $mission_car_2 in_current_position 1
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #POLICE
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #COP
fade 1 500
0@ = 0
1@ = 0
TIMERA = 0
if
    $mission_debug == 0
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_SCENE_1_SKIP

:POLICE_1_SCENE_1
wait 0
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_1 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.45 -0.85 0.25
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_2 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.4 -0.95 0.2
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_3 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.35 -1.65 0.15
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_4 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.45 -1.85 0.3
place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_5 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.0 -1.1 0.9
if and
    0@ == 0
    TIMERA >= 2000
then
    set_fixed_camera_position -841.5286 -634.7706 13.1116 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
    point_camera_at_point -843.3661 -634.0018 11.504 switchstyle 2
    0@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    0@ == 1
    TIMERA >= 1500
then
    set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 2000
    point_camera_at_char $mission_actor_1 mode 15 switchstyle 1
    0@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    0@ == 2
    TIMERA >= 2000
then
    char_look_at_char_always $mission_actor_1 to_look_at_actor $player_actor
    0@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    0@ == 3
    TIMERA >= 500
then
    char_look_at_char_always $player_actor to_look_at_actor $mission_actor_1
    set_char_wait_state $player_actor anim 19 wait_state_time 1500
    print_now 'SCENE1' time 1800 1
    0@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    0@ == 4
    TIMERA >= 2000
then
    set_fixed_camera_position -841.4791 -640.2056 11.1239 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
    point_camera_at_char $mission_actor_2 mode 15 switchstyle 2
    set_char_obj_run_to_coord $mission_actor_2 run_to -841.0 -635.0
    stop_char_looking $player_actor
    stop_char_looking $mission_actor_1
    turn_char_to_face_char $player_actor look_at_actor $mission_actor_1
    turn_char_to_face_char $mission_actor_1 look_at_actor $player_actor
    set_char_wait_state $player_actor anim 19 wait_state_time 10000
    set_char_wait_state $mission_actor_1 anim 19 wait_state_time 10000
    0@++
    TIMERA = 0
end
if
    0@ == 5
then
    if
        is_char_objective_passed $mission_actor_2
    then
        set_char_obj_enter_car_as_driver $mission_actor_2 go_to_and_drive_car $objective_car
        set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 3000
        set_fixed_camera_position -841.4791 -640.2056 12.1239 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
        point_camera_at_char $player_actor mode 15 switchstyle 1
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
    end
    if
        TIMERA > 3000
    then
        goto @POLICE_1_SCENE_1_SKIP
    end
end
if
    0@ == 6
then
    if
        TIMERA > 1000
    then
        clear_all_char_anims $player_actor
        clear_all_char_anims $mission_actor_1
        turn_char_to_face_char $mission_actor_1 look_at_actor $mission_actor_2
        char_look_at_char_always $mission_actor_1 to_look_at_actor $mission_actor_2
        turn_char_to_face_char $player_actor look_at_actor $mission_actor_2
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
    end
end
if
    0@ == 7
then
    if
        TIMERA > 1000
    then
        stop_char_looking $player_actor
        set_char_obj_enter_car_as_driver $player_actor go_to_and_drive_car $mission_car
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
    end
end
if
    0@ == 8
then
    if
        is_char_in_car $player_actor in_car $mission_car
    then
        0@++
    end
    if
        TIMERA > 3000
    then
        goto @POLICE_1_SCENE_1_SKIP
    end
end
if and
    is_char_in_car $mission_actor_2 in_car $objective_car
    1@ == 0
then
    set_car_cruise_speed $objective_car max_speed_to 100.0
    car_goto_coordinates_accurate $objective_car drive_to_point -832.6553 -667.8333 10.934
    1@ = 1
end
if
    0@ == 9
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_SCENE_1
goto @POLICE_1_SCENE_1_END

:POLICE_1_SCENE_1_SKIP
stop_char_looking $player_actor
clear_all_char_anims $player_actor
warp_char_into_car $player_actor in_car $mission_car
warp_char_into_car $mission_actor_2 in_car $objective_car
restore_camera_jumpcut

:POLICE_1_SCENE_1_END
delete_char $mission_actor_1
freeze_car_position $mission_car in_current_position 0
set_car_proofs $mission_car immunities 0 0 0 0 0
set_can_burst_car_tyres $mission_car tires_vulnerable 1
lock_car_doors $objective_car door_status_to 3
set_car_heavy $objective_car very_heavy 1
switch_widescreen 0
set_interpolation_parameters 0.0 1000
restore_camera
set_camera_behind_player
set_player_control $player_char can_move 1
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 0
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 0
set_car_proofs $objective_car immunities 1 1 1 1 1
set_car_heavy $objective_car very_heavy 1
set_car_cruise_speed $objective_car max_speed_to 100.0
set_car_driving_style $objective_car traffic_behavior_to 3
set_car_coordinates $objective_car at -835.6672 -635.2399 9.6925
set_car_heading $objective_car z_angle_to 190.6025
set_car_forward_speed $objective_car speed_instantly 10.0
set_car_traction $objective_car improve_handling 2.0
car_goto_coordinates_accurate $objective_car drive_to_point -824.6089 -895.7141 11.0995
add_blip_for_car $objective_car_marker = create_marker_above_car $objective_car
print_now 'CATCH' time 5000 2
0@ = 0
1@ = 0
if
    $mission_debug == 1
then
    set_car_coordinates $objective_car at -824.6 -890.7 10.0
    set_car_heading $objective_car z_angle_to 180.0
    set_car_coordinates $mission_car at -824.6 -885.7 10.0
    set_car_heading $mission_car z_angle_to 180.0
end

:POLICE_1_CHASE
wait 0
if
    not is_car_dead $objective_car
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_WRECKED
if
    not locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car $objective_car radius 100.0 100.0 0
then
    print_now 'CATCHF' time 5000 2
    goto @POLICE_1_FAIL
end
if
    0@ <> 10
then
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_1 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.45 -0.85 0.25
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_2 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.4 -0.95 0.2
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_3 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.35 -1.65 0.15
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_4 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.45 -1.85 0.3
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_5 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.0 -1.1 0.9
end
if
    0@ == 0
then
    if
        locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car $objective_car radius 20.0 20.0 0
    then
        set_car_cruise_speed $objective_car max_speed_to 100.0
    else
        set_car_cruise_speed $objective_car max_speed_to 25.0
    end
end
if and
    0@ == 0
    locate_car_2d $objective_car sphere 0 near_point -824.6089 -895.7141 radius 50.0 50.0
then
    freeze_car_position $mission_car_2 in_current_position 0
    set_car_forward_speed $mission_car_2 speed_instantly 20.0
    set_car_cruise_speed $mission_car_2 max_speed_to 100.0
    set_car_driving_style $mission_car_2 traffic_behavior_to 3
    set_car_straight_line_distance $mission_car_2 abandon_path_radius 255
    car_goto_coordinates_accurate $mission_car_2 drive_to_point -820.8316 -896.5915 10.9268
    set_car_cruise_speed $objective_car max_speed_to 100.0
    0@ = 1
end
if and
    0@ == 1
    locate_car_2d $objective_car sphere 0 near_point -824.6089 -895.7141 radius 10.0 10.0
then
    set_car_proofs $objective_car immunities 0 0 0 0 0
    set_car_heavy $objective_car very_heavy 0
    get_car_health 1@ = car $objective_car
    1@--
    0@ = 2
end
if and
    not is_car_health_greater $objective_car health > 1@
    0@ > 0
    10 > 0@
then
    set_char_obj_flee_player_on_foot_always $mission_actor_2 avoid_player $player_char
    set_car_straight_line_distance $mission_car_2 abandon_path_radius 3
    car_goto_coordinates_accurate $mission_car_2 drive_to_point 0.0 0.0 0.0
    set_car_density_multiplier 1.0
    set_ped_density_multiplier 1.0
    delete_object $mission_obj_1
    delete_object $mission_obj_2
    delete_object $mission_obj_3
    delete_object $mission_obj_4
    delete_object $mission_obj_5
    create_object $mission_obj_1 = create_object #GUNBOX at 0.0 0.0 0.0
    create_object $mission_obj_2 = create_object #CARDBOARDBOX2 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
    create_object $mission_obj_3 = create_object #CARDBOARDBOX2 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
    create_object $mission_obj_4 = create_object #GUNBOX at 0.0 0.0 0.0
    create_object $mission_obj_5 = create_object #CARDBOARDBOX2 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_1 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.7 -0.8 0.5
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_2 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.7 -0.8 0.5
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_3 relative_to_car $objective_car offset -0.7 -1.8 0.5
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_4 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.7 -1.8 0.5
    place_object_relative_to_car $mission_obj_5 relative_to_car $objective_car offset 0.0 -1.1 1.0
    set_object_velocity $mission_obj_1 distance -5.0 0.0 10.0
    set_object_velocity $mission_obj_2 distance 5.0 0.0 10.0
    set_object_velocity $mission_obj_3 distance 0.0 -5.0 10.0
    set_object_velocity $mission_obj_4 distance -5.0 5.0 10.0
    set_object_velocity $mission_obj_5 distance 5.0 5.0 10.0
    set_can_burst_car_tyres $objective_car tires_vulnerable 1
    burst_car_tyre $objective_car deflate_tire 1
    burst_car_tyre $objective_car deflate_tire 2
    set_car_traction $objective_car improve_handling 1.0
    lock_car_doors $objective_car door_status_to 1
    set_car_health $objective_car health_to 400
    0@ = 10
    TIMERA = 0
end
if and
    0@ == 10
    TIMERA > 2000
goto_if_false @POLICE_1_CHASE
set_player_control $player_char can_move 0
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 1
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 1
remove_blip $objective_car_marker
fade 0 500
wait 500
set_car_coordinates $objective_car at -823.3806 -892.7518 9.7753
set_car_heading $objective_car z_angle_to 170.081
set_car_health $objective_car health_to 400
set_car_coordinates $mission_car at -820.9627 -884.8602 9.6969
set_car_heading $mission_car z_angle_to 203.0539
set_car_coordinates $mission_car_2 at -797.4353 -897.4156 9.9078
set_car_heading $mission_car_2 z_angle_to 358.8944
switch_widescreen 1
set_fixed_camera_position -813.3096 -898.5632 11.0903 rotation 0.0 0.0 0.0
point_camera_at_car $objective_car mode 15 switchstyle 2
delete_object $mission_obj_1
delete_object $mission_obj_2
delete_object $mission_obj_3
delete_object $mission_obj_4
delete_object $mission_obj_5
create_object $mission_obj_1 = create_object #CARDBOARDBOX2 at -824.9583 -887.8648 10.1002

const cm_spawn_distance = 125.0
const cm_despawn_distance = 150.0

:CAR_MECHANIC_LOOP
wait 0
if
    is_car_dead $mission_car
then
    clear_prints
    print_now 'CMFAIL3' time 5000 1 // ~r~You destroyed our truck! You're fired.
    goto @CAR_MECHANIC_FAIL
end
if
    1 > $mission_timer
then
    clear_prints
    print_now 'CMFAIL2' time 5000 1 // ~r~You are out of time. You're fired.
    goto @CAR_MECHANIC_FAIL
end
if
    is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 19
then
    $cm_cancel_button_pressed = 1
end
if and
    $cm_cancel_button_pressed == 1
    not is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 19
then
    clear_prints
    print_now 'CMCANCL' time 5000 1 // ~r~Car Mechanic mission cancelled!
    goto @CAR_MECHANIC_FAIL
end
if and
    $cm_hint_shown == 0
    TIMERA > 10000
then
    print_help 'CMHINT'
    $cm_hint_shown = 1
end
$near_any_mission_car = 0
if
    $mission_car_1_broken > 0
then
    if
        $mission_car_1_visible == 0
    then
        if and
            locate_player_any_means_2d $player_char 0 $mission_car_1_x $mission_car_1_y radius cm_spawn_distance cm_spawn_distance
            is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $mission_car
        then
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 0@ = $mission_car_1_x
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 1@ = $mission_car_1_y
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 2@ = $mission_car_1_z
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 3@ = $mission_car_1_angle
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 4@ = $mission_car_1_model
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 5@ = $mission_car_1_actor_model
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 6@ = $mission_car_1_type
            CAR_MECHANIC_CREATE_CAR()
            set_var_int_to_lvar_int $mission_car_1 = 14@
            set_var_int_to_lvar_int $mission_car_1_driver = 15@
            $mission_car_1_visible = 1
        end
    else
        if
            not locate_player_any_means_car_2d $player_char near_car $mission_car_1 radius cm_despawn_distance cm_despawn_distance 0
        then
            delete_char $mission_car_1_driver
            delete_car $mission_car_1
            $mission_car_1_visible = 0
        else
            if and
                not is_car_dead $mission_car_1
                not is_char_dead $mission_car_1_driver
            goto_if_false @CAR_MECHANIC_WRECKED
            if
                is_char_in_car $mission_car_1_driver in_car $mission_car_1
            goto_if_false @CAR_MECHANIC_WRECKED
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 0@ = $mission_car_1
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 1@ = $mission_car_1_driver
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 2@ = $mission_car_1_type
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 3@ = $mission_car_1_broken
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 4@ = $mission_car_1_interacted
            set_lvar_int_to_var_int 5@ = $mission_car_1_health
            CAR_MECHANIC_CAR_VISIBLE()
            set_var_int_to_lvar_int $mission_car_1_broken = 3@
            set_var_int_to_lvar_int $mission_car_1_interacted = 4@
            set_var_int_to_lvar_int $mission_car_1_health = 5@
            if
                15@ == 1
            then
                remove_blip $mission_car_1_marker
                $mission_car_1_visible = 0
            end
        end
    end
end

then

        goto @CAR_MECHANIC_FAIL
    end
    if
        has_car_been_damaged_by_weapon $mission_car hit_by_weapon 7
    then
        clear_car_last_weapon_damage $mission_car

            not is_wanted_level_greater $player_char wanted_level > 1

        end
        if
            $cm_barrel <> -1
        then
            delete_object $cm_barrel
        end
        request_model #BARREL4
        while not has_model_loaded #BARREL4
            wait 0
        end
        get_offset_from_car_in_world_coords 0@ 1@ 2@ from_car $mission_car offset 0.0 -2.7 -0.5
        create_object $cm_barrel = create_object #BARREL4 at 0@ 1@ 2@
        set_object_dynamic $cm_barrel toggle_in_moving_list 1
        get_car_heading 2@ = car $mission_car
        2@ -= 180.0
        cos 0@ = cosine 2@
        sin 1@ = sine 2@
        0@ *= 2.0
        1@ *= 2.0
        add_to_object_velocity $cm_barrel scatter 0@ 1@ 1.0
    end
else
    $mission_objective_shown = 0
    if
        not is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $mission_car

            $mission_car_marker_active == 0

            print_now 'CMBACK' time 5000 1 // ~g~Return to the truck.
            $mission_car_marker_active = 1
        end
    else
        if
            $mission_car_marker_active == 1
        then
            remove_blip $mission_car_marker
            clear_this_print 'CMBACK' // ~g~Return to the truck.
            $mission_car_marker_active = 0
        end
    end

        $cm_repair_meter_shown == 1

        $cm_repair_meter_shown = 0

    $cm_barrel <> -1

        has_object_been_damaged $cm_barrel
        not locate_char_any_means_object_2d $player_actor object $cm_barrel radius 50.0 50.0 flag 0
    then

        $cm_barrel = -1
    else
        if and
            locate_char_any_means_object_3d $player_actor object $cm_barrel radius 1.0 1.0 1.0 flag 0
            TIMERA > 500
        then
            get_player_coordinates $player_char position_to 0@ 1@ 2@
            get_object_coordinates $cm_barrel position_to 3@ 4@ 5@
            sub_float_lvar_from_float_lvar 3@ -= 0@
            sub_float_lvar_from_float_lvar 4@ -= 1@
            3@ *= 5.0
            4@ *= 5.0
            add_to_object_velocity $cm_barrel scatter 3@ 4@ 1.0
            TIMERA = 0
        end
    end
end
if and
    0 >= $mission_car_1_broken
    0 >= $mission_car_2_broken

    12@ > 300.0

    13@ > 650.0

:CAR_MECHANIC_CREATE_CAR_LOADED
create_car 14@ = create_car 4@ at 0@ 1@ 2@
set_car_heading 14@ z_angle_to 3@
create_char_inside_car 15@ = create_actor 4 5@ in_car 14@
car_set_idle 14@
if
    6@ == 1
then
    set_car_health 14@ health_to 400
end
boat_stop 14@
set_car_only_damaged_by_player 14@ immune_to_nonplayer 1
set_char_only_damaged_by_player 15@ immune_to_nonplayer 1
return

:CAR_MECHANIC_CAR_VISIBLE
15@ = 0
get_car_coordinates 0@ position_to 6@ 7@ 8@
if and
    $near_any_mission_car == 0
    locate_car_2d $mission_car sphere 0 near_point 6@ 7@ radius 20.0 20.0
then
    $near_any_mission_car = 1
    if
        $mission_objective_shown == 0
    then
        $mission_objective_shown = 1
        CAR_MECHANIC_SHOW_OBJECTIVE()
        if
            2@ <> 3
        then
            $cm_repair_meter_value = 0
            display_nth_onscreen_counter_with_string $cm_repair_meter_value 1 line 1 'CMMETER' // Repair:
            $cm_repair_meter_shown = 1
            set_var_int_to_lvar_int $cm_repair_meter_total = 3@
        end
        remove_blip $mission_car_current_marker
        add_blip_for_car_old $mission_car_current_marker = create_marker_above_car 0@ color 0 display 1
        $mission_car_current_marker_active = 1
    end
end
if
    2@ == 1
then
    if
        has_car_been_damaged_by_weapon 0@ hit_by_weapon 7
    then
        clear_car_last_weapon_damage 0@
        if
            not is_wanted_level_greater $player_char wanted_level > 1
        then
            clear_wanted_level $player_char
        end
        get_car_health 5@ = car 0@
        3@--
        if
            3@ > 0
        then
            add_one_off_sound 13 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
        else
            add_one_off_sound 1 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
        end
        car_wander_randomly 0@
        TIMERA = 0
        4@ = 1

        set_var_int_to_var_int $cm_repair_meter_value = $cm_repair_meter_total
        sub_int_lvar_from_int_var $cm_repair_meter_value += 3@
        $cm_repair_meter_value *= 100
        div_int_var_by_int_var $cm_repair_meter_value /= $cm_repair_meter_total
    end
    if and
        4@ == 1
        TIMERA > 200
    then
        boat_stop 0@
        4@ = 0
    end
else
    if
        2@ == 2
    then
        get_car_speed 14@ = car 0@
        if and
            14@ > 0.5
            locate_player_in_car_car_2d $player_char near_car 0@ radius 7.0 7.0 0
        then
            if
                4@ == 0
            then
                TIMERA = 0
                add_one_off_sound 13 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
            end
            4@ = 1
        else
            if
                4@ == 1
            then
                4@ = 2
                TIMERB = 0
            end
            if and
                4@ == 2
                TIMERB > 200
            then
                4@ = 0
                $cm_repair_meter_value = 0
                add_one_off_sound 14 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
            end
        end
        if
            4@ <> 0
        then
            set_var_int_to_lvar_int $cm_repair_meter_value = TIMERA
            $cm_repair_meter_value *= 100
            $cm_repair_meter_value /= 2250
            if
                TIMERA > 2250
            then
                3@ = 0
                add_one_off_sound 1 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
            end
        end
    else
        if
            $cm_barrel <> -1
        then
            get_car_coordinates 0@ position_to 12@ 13@ 14@
            if
                locate_object_3d $cm_barrel near_point 12@ 13@ 14@ radius 1.4 1.4 1.4 flag 0
            then
                delete_object $cm_barrel
                $cm_barrel = -1
                3@ = 0
                add_one_off_sound 1 at 0.0 0.0 0.0
            end
        end
    end
end
if
    0 >= 3@
then
    set_car_health 0@ health_to 1000
    CAR_MECHANIC_FIXED()
    4@ = 0
    15@ = 1
    remove_blip $mission_car_current_marker
    $mission_car_current_marker_active = 0
else
    get_car_health 14@ = car 0@
    if
        is_int_var_greater_than_int_lvar 5@ > 14@
    then
        set_var_int_to_lvar_int 5@ = 14@
        CAR_MECHANIC_FINE()
    end
end
return

:CAR_MECHANIC_SHOW_OBJECTIVE
if
    2@ == 1
then
    print_now 'BROKEN1' time 5000 1 // ~g~The engine is broken. Use the ~h~hammer~g~ tool to fix it.
else
    if
        2@ == 2
    then
        print_now 'BROKEN2' time 5000 1 // ~g~The car's stuck. ~h~Push~g~ it with ~y~the truck~g~ to start the engine. Be careful!
    else
        print_now 'BROKEN3' time 5000 1 // ~g~The car's out of fule. Use the ~h~hammer~g~ tool to get fuel from ~y~the truck~g~.
    end
end
return

:CAR_MECHANIC_FINE
add_score $player_char money += -50
print_with_number_big 'CMFINE' number 50 time 1000 style 4 // ~r~$~1~ damage fine
return

return

end

return

    if and

        TIMERA > 5000
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0

    if and

        TIMERA > 3500

        0@++
        TIMERA = 0

        TIMERA > 3000

        0@++
        TIMERA = 0

    if and
        0@ == 8
        TIMERA > 4500
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO7' time 5500 1

    end

        switch_widescreen 0
        restore_camera_jumpcut
        set_camera_behind_player
    end
end
if
    $mission_step == 2
then
    draw_corona 2.5 type 6 lensflares 0 with_color 255 137 205 at 12.0997 963.1759 15.954
    if
        is_player_in_car $player_char $objective_car
    then
        if
            0@ == 1
        then
            remove_blip $objective_car_marker
        end
        if
            locate_player_in_car_2d $player_char 1 16.4823 962.6206 radius 3.0 3.0
        then
            jump @POLICE_2_ESCAPED
        end
    else
        if
            0@ == 0
        then
            add_blip_for_car $objective_car_marker = create_marker_above_car $objective_car
        end
    end
    if and
        1@ == 1
        is_player_in_car $player_char $mission_car_1
    then
        remove_blip $mission_car_1_marker
    end
end
goto @POLICE_2_ESCAPE

:POLICE_2_ESCAPED
clear_onscreen_timer $mission_timer
mark_car_as_no_longer_needed $mission_car_1
mark_car_as_no_longer_needed $mission_car_2
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_1
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_2
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_3
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_4
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_5
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_6
remove_blip $mission_car_1_marker
remove_blip $objective_car_marker
remove_blip $objective_point_marker
add_blip_for_coord $objective_point_marker = create_checkpoint_at 502.5375 502.7857 10.9967
print_now 'FREEDOM' time 5000 2
0@ = 1

:POLICE_2_TRAVEL_2
wait 0
if
    not is_car_dead $objective_car
goto_if_false @POLICE_2_WRECKED
if
    0@ == 0
then
    if
        is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $objective_car
    goto_if_false @POLICE_2_TRAVEL_2
    remove_blip $objective_car_marker
    add_blip_for_coord $objective_point_marker = create_checkpoint_at 502.5375 502.7857 10.9967
    0@ = 1
else
    if
        not is_player_in_car $player_char in_car $objective_car
    then
        print_now 'GETBACK' time 5000 2
        remove_blip $objective_point_marker
        add_blip_for_car $objective_car_marker = create_marker_above_car $objective_car
        0@ = 0
        jump @POLICE_2_TRAVEL_2
    end
    if
        not locate_stopped_player_in_car_2d $player_char stopped 1 502.5375 502.7857 radius 4.0 4.0
    goto_if_false @POLICE_2_TRAVEL_2_END
end
jump @POLICE_2_TRAVEL_2

:POLICE_2_TRAVEL_2_END
remove_blip $objective_point_marker
clear_prints
set_player_control $player_char 0
fade 0 500
wait 1000
clear_extra_colours 0
switch_widescreen 1
set_fixed_camera_position 507.5866 508.2696 11.8487 0.0 0.0 0.0
point_camera_at_point 504.4974 505.9874 11.3646 2
set_car_coordinates $objective_car 502.5375 502.7857 10.1967
set_car_heading $objective_car 180.5382
warp_player_from_car_to_coord $player_char 505.3627 505.3947 10.3479
set_char_heading $player_actor 99.4804
request_model #VICE3
load_all_models_now
create_char $mission_actor_1 4 #VICE3 496.7986 505.9915 10.3995
set_char_heading $mission_actor_1 270.0
set_char_obj_run_to_coord $mission_actor_1 501.7986 505.9915
fade 1 1000
15@ = 0
TIMERA = 0
while True
    wait 0
    if
        15@ == 0
    then
        if or
            is_char_objective_passed $mission_actor_1
            TIMERA > 5000
        then
            15@++
            TIMERA = 0
            print_now 'OUTRO1' time 3000 1
        end
    end
    if and
        15@ == 1
        TIMERA > 3000
    then
        15@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'OUTRO2' time 3000 1
    end
    if and
        15@ == 2
        TIMERA > 3000
    then
        15@++
        TIMERA = 0
        set_fixed_camera_position 504.7986 506.9915 12.3995 0.0 0.0 0.0
        point_camera_at_point 501.7986 505.9915 11.8995 2
        print_now 'OUTRO3' time 2500 1
    end
    if and
        15@ == 3
        TIMERA > 2500
    then
        15@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'OUTRO4' time 4000 1
    end
    if and
        15@ == 4
        TIMERA > 4000
    then
        break
    end
    if
        not is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 16
    then
        14@ = 1
    end
    if and
        14@ == 1
        is_button_pressed 0 pressed_button 16
    then
        break
    end
end
fade 0 1000
wait 1000
clear_prints
delete_car $objective_car
delete_char $mission_actor_1
fade 1 1000
set_player_control $player_char 1
switch_widescreen 0
restore_camera_jumpcut
set_camera_behind_player
goto @POLICE_2_PASS

:POLICE_2_TIMEOUT
print_now 'TIMEOUT' time 5000 1
POLICE_2_FAIL()
return

:POLICE_2_SPOTTED
print_now 'SPOTTED' time 5000 1
POLICE_2_FAIL()
return

:POLICE_2_WRECKED
print_now 'CARF' time 5000 2
POLICE_2_FAIL()
return

:POLICE_2_WHY
print_now 'WHY' time 5000 1
POLICE_2_FAIL()
return

:POLICE_2_FAIL
print_big 'M_FAIL' 5000 ms 1 // MISSION FAILED!
return

:POLICE_2_PASS
play_mission_passed_tune 1
print_with_number_big 'M_PASS' number 1000 time 5000 style 1 // MISSION PASSED! $~1~
add_score $player_char money += 1000
register_mission_passed 'POLIC2S'
player_made_progress 1
$passed_police_2 = 1
remove_blip $icon_police
switch_car_generator $police_car_spawn cars_to_generate_to 101
return

:POLICE_2_CLEANUP
$onmission = 0
$npcs_north_island_allowed = 1
$allow_police_chases = 1
flash_hud_object -1
mark_car_as_no_longer_needed $objective_car
mark_car_as_no_longer_needed $mission_car_1
mark_car_as_no_longer_needed $mission_car_2
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_1
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_2
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_3
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_4
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_5
remove_char_elegantly $mission_actor_6
remove_blip $mission_actor_1_marker
remove_blip $mission_actor_2_marker
remove_blip $mission_actor_3_marker
remove_blip $mission_actor_4_marker
remove_blip $mission_actor_5_marker
remove_blip $mission_actor_6_marker
remove_blip $mission_car_1_marker
remove_blip $objective_car_marker
remove_blip $objective_point_marker
remove_blip $mission_obj_1_marker
remove_blip $mission_obj_2_marker
remove_blip $mission_obj_3_marker
remove_blip $mission_obj_4_marker
delete_object $mission_obj_1
delete_object $mission_obj_2
delete_object $mission_obj_3
delete_object $mission_obj_4
remove_pickup $mission_weapon_pickup_1
remove_script_fire $mission_fire_1
remove_script_fire $mission_fire_2
remove_script_fire $mission_fire_3
remove_script_fire $mission_fire_4
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #POLICE
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #PACKER
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #WALTON
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #VICE3
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #WMYRI
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #HMYRI
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #COLT45
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #UZI
mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BARREL4
clear_onscreen_timer $mission_timer
clear_onscreen_counter $notice_counter
set_player_is_in_stadium 0
clear_extra_colours 0
mission_has_finished
return

//-------------Mission 6---------------
// The Clearout

:BIKER_1
script_name 'BIKER1'
gosub @BIKER_1_START
if
    has_deatharrest_been_executed
then
    BIKER_1_FAIL()
end
BIKER_1_CLEANUP()
terminate_this_script

:BIKER_1_START
$onmission = 1
set_fading_colour 0 0 0
register_mission_given
load_mission_text 'BIKER1'
set_player_control $player_char 0
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 1
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 1
fade 0 500
wait 500
switch_widescreen 1
clear_area 0 at -600.1636 652.1155 10.1262 range 20.0
set_car_density_multiplier 0.0
set_ped_density_multiplier 0.0
set_char_coordinates $player_actor -600.5449 653.8733 10.0721
set_char_heading $player_actor 180.0
if
    is_char_dead $npc_biker_1
then
    delete_char $npc_biker_1
    request_model #BKB
    load_all_models_now
    NPCS_BIKERS_CREATE_GUARD()
    mark_model_as_no_longer_needed #BKB
end
set_fixed_camera_position -603.6945 655.5886 12.0735 0.0 0.0 0.0
point_camera_at_char $npc_biker_1 15 2
set_char_wait_state $npc_biker_1 anim 19 wait_state_time 1000000
fade 1 1000
0@ = 0
TIMERA = 0
while True
    wait 0
    if and
        0@ == 0
        TIMERA > 1000
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO1' time 2500 1
    end
    if and
        0@ == 1
        TIMERA > 2500
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO2' time 5000 1
    end
    if and
        0@ == 2
        TIMERA > 5000
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO3' time 7000 1
    end
    if and
        0@ == 3
        TIMERA > 7000
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO4' time 4500 1
    end
    if and
        0@ == 4
        TIMERA > 4500
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO5' time 6000 1
    end
    if and
        0@ == 5
        TIMERA > 6000
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO6' time 6500 1
    end
    if and
        0@ == 6
        TIMERA > 6500
    then
        0@++
        TIMERA = 0
        print_now 'INTRO7' time 6500 1
    end
    if and
        0@ == 7
        TIMERA > 6500
    then
        break
    end
    if or
        {$I incl.anykey.txt}
    then
        if
            0@ > 0
        then
            break
        end
    end
end
fade 0 500
wait 500
clear_all_char_anims $npc_biker_1
if
    $npcs_bikers_state == 0
then
    remove_char_elegantly $npc_biker_1
end
clear_prints
set_player_coordinates $player_char -515.7791 686.6896 10.0728
set_player_heading $player_char 282.0751
set_player_control $player_char 1
set_police_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_cops_state_to 0
set_everyone_ignore_player $player_char ignored_by_everyone_to 0
set_car_density_multiplier 1.0
set_ped_density_multiplier 1.0
switch_widescreen 0
restore_camera_jumpcut
set_camera_behind_player
fade 1 500
wait 1000
return

:BIKER_1_WRECKED
print_now 'CARF' time 5000 2
BIKER_1_FAIL()
return

:BIKER_1_FAIL
print_big 'M_FAIL' 5000 ms 1 // MISSION FAILED!
return

:BIKER_1_PASS
play_mission_passed_tune 1
print_with_number_big 'M_PASS' number 250 time 5000 style 1 // MISSION PASSED! $~1~
add_score $player_char money += 250
register_mission_passed 'BIKER1S'
player_made_progress 1
$passed_biker_1 = 1
remove_blip $icon_biker
return

:BIKER_1_CLEANUP
$onmission = 0
mark_car_as_no_longer_needed $mission_car_1
remove_blip $mission_car_1_marker
remove_blip $objective_point_marker
remove_blip $mission_obj_1_marker
delete_object $mission_obj_1
mission_has_finished
return
